Note: Many more in-depth descriptions of Ogre subdirectories and contents can be found at http://www.ogre3d.org/wiki/index.php/Main_Page
Note 2: Ogre subdirectories already include many things pertaining to Linux, OS X, and OpenGL, so transferring rendering may be easier than expected.

Smoke
|-- bin - Contains Subdirectories which contain DLL files for both Release and Debug 
|   |     Versions, Also contains various .cdf, .odf, .gdf, .sdf, and .odf file
|   |
|   |-- debug -  Contains DLL files (Microsofts type of Shared Libraries)
|   |   |-- OgreMain_d.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_BSPSceneManager_d.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_CgProgramManager_d.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_OctreeSceneManager_d.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_ParticleFX_d.dll
|   |   |-- RenderSystem_Direct3D9_d.dll
|   |   |-- cg.dll
|   |   |-- fmodex.dll
|   |   |-- tbb_debug.dll
|   |   `-- tbbmalloc_debug.dll
|   |
|   |-- logs - Contains log files (Plaintext log of events and timestamps)
|   |   `-- empty.log
|   |
|   |-- profile -  Contains DLL files (Microsofts type of Shared Libraries)
|   |   |-- OgreMain.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_BSPSceneManager.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_CgProgramManager.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_OctreeSceneManager.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_ParticleFX.dll
|   |   |-- RenderSystem_Direct3D9.dll
|   |   |-- cg.dll
|   |   |-- fmodex.dll
|   |   |-- tbb.dll
|   |   `-- tbbmalloc.dll
|   |
|   |-- release  -  Contains DLL files (Microsofts type of Shared Libraries)
|   |   |-- OgreMain.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_BSPSceneManager.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_CgProgramManager.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_OctreeSceneManager.dll
|   |   |-- Plugin_ParticleFX.dll
|   |   |-- RenderSystem_Direct3D9.dll
|   |   |-- cg.dll
|   |   |-- fmodex.dll
|   |   |-- tbb.dll
|   |   `-- tbbmalloc.dll
|   |
|   |-- Audio.sdf
|   |-- Ball.odf
|   |-- Birds.cdf
|   |-- Chicken.odf
|   |-- ColdParticle.odf
|   |-- Demo.cdf
|   |-- Demo_House.cdf
|   |-- Demo_Shingles_Boxy.cdf
|   |-- Demo_Shingles_Foxy.cdf
|   |-- Demo_Swallows.cdf
|   |-- Demo_TreesAndFire.cdf
|   |-- FireBall.odf
|   |-- FireCanopyA.odf
|   |-- FireCanopyEmbers.odf
|   |-- FireCanopyFire.odf

|   |-- Graphics.sdf
|   |-- Horse.odf

|-- code - Contains all files needed to build the Smoke Program
|   |
|   |-- build info - Contains Instructions for building under Windows
|   |   `-- build.txt
|   |
|   |-- extern - Contains files pertaining to external Libraries E.G Havok, Ogre, etc.
|   |   |
|   |   |-- FMOD - Contains files for the FMOD Audio Engine
